   A) 4
   B) 5
   C) 7
   D) 10

78. A computer generates random numbers uniformly between 1 and 50. What is the probability of generating a number greater than 40?
   A) 0.1
   B) 0.2
   C) 0.25
   D) 0.3

79. A bag contains 5 red balls and 3 blue balls. Two balls are drawn at random without replacement. What is the probability that one ball is red and the other is blue?
   A) 15/56
   B) 30/56
   C) 25/56
   D) 35/56

80. A dataset has values {100, 105, 110, 115, 120}. Calculate the coefficient of variation (CV).
   A) 4.08%
   B) 4.33%
   C) 5.00%
   D) 5.12%



--- CORRECT ANSWERS AND EXPLANATIONS ---

1. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: The probability of a product being defective is 5% (0.05). Therefore, the probability of the product not being defective is 1 - 0.05 = 0.95.

2. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: There are 6 possible pairs of outcomes that result in a sum of 7: (1,6), (2,5), (3,4), (4,3), (5,2), (6,1). Since there are 36 total outcomes, the probability is 6/36 = 5/36.

3. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: For a normal distribution, 68% of the data falls within one standard deviation of the mean.

4. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Stratified sampling divides the population into subgroups (strata) and then samples randomly within each subgroup to ensure representation.

5. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: For independent events, P(A and B) = P(A) × P(B). Therefore, P(A and B) = 0.4 × 0.5 = 0.2.

6. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: The number of arrangements is calculated using factorials: 5! = 5 × 4 × 3 × 2 × 1 = 120.

7. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: Bayes’ theorem is used to compute this. For simplicity, the calculations yield approximately 0.167.

8. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: If the median is greater than the mean, the distribution is skewed left, meaning there are lower values pulling the mean down.

9. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: R-squared measures the proportion of variability in the dependent variable that can be explained by the independent variable.

10. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: The expected value is calculated as the sum of all outcomes multiplied by their probabilities: (1+2+3+4+5+6)/6 = 3.5.

11. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: The area under the probability density function curve for a continuous probability distribution is always equal to 1.

12. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: Using the multiplication rule: P(A and B) = P(A) × P(B | A). Therefore, P(A and B) = 0.3 × 0.4 = 0.12.

13. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: A random variable assigns numerical values to the outcomes of a stochastic process or experiment.

14. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: The null hypothesis assumes no effect or no difference, and it is tested against the alternative hypothesis.

15. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: The Central Limit Theorem states that, regardless of the population distribution shape, the sampling distribution of the sample mean becomes approximately normal as the sample size grows.

16. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: Variance measures the spread of data and is always non-negative, as it is based on squared deviations.

17. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: Using the formula for conditional probability: P(A and B) = P(A) × P(B | A). Thus, P(A and B) = 0.6 × 0.5 = 0.3.

18. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: The expected value for a binomial random variable is given by E(X) = n × p. Thus, E(X) = 10 × 0.3 = 3.

19. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: In a standard normal distribution, the mean is 0. Therefore, the probability of a value being less than the mean is 50%.

20. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: Covariance is positive when the two variables show similar directional tendencies, either increasing or decreasing together.

21. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: The possible pairs to achieve a sum of 7 are (1,6), (2,5), (3,4), (4,3), (5,2), and (6,1). There are 6 outcomes out of 36 total possible outcomes from two dice rolls, so the probability is 6/36 = 1/6.

22. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: To find the mean, sum all values and divide by the number of data points. (4 + 7 + 9 + 11 + 15) / 5 = 46 / 5 = 9.2.

23. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: There are 10 balls total, and 5 are red. The probability of selecting a red ball is 5/10 = 1/2.

24. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: Z-score is calculated as (X - mean) / standard deviation = (60 - 50) / 5 = 10 / 5 = 2.

25. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: The expected value is calculated as the sum of each outcome multiplied by its probability. Each side has equal probability (1/6), so E = (1+2+3+4+5+6)/6 = 21/6 = 3.5.

26. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: Standard deviation is the square root of variance. √25 = 5.

27. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: For independent events, P(A and B) = P(A) × P(B). Therefore, P(A and B) = 0.4 × 0.5 = 0.2.

28. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: The median is the middle value when the data is ordered. Here, the sorted dataset is {8, 12, 15, 20, 30}, and the middle value is 15.

29. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: The probability of failure is 1 - reliability = 1 - 0.95 = 0.05.

30. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Positive skewness indicates that the tail extends to the right side of the distribution.

31. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: Each coin has a probability of 1/2 for heads. For two coins, P = 1/2 × 1/2 = 1/4.

32. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: The mode is the most frequently occurring value. Here, 20 appears twice, making it the mode.

33. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: The complement is the probability of getting no heads, which is (1/2)^3 = 1/8. Therefore, P(at least one heads) = 1 - 1/8 = 7/8.

34. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: Range is calculated as the difference between the maximum and minimum values: 15 - 3 = 12.

35. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: For mutually exclusive events, P(A or B) = P(A) + P(B). Therefore, P(A or B) = 0.3 + 0.5 = 0.8.

36. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: If the mean is greater than the median, the distribution is positively skewed.

37. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: P(A) = number of outcomes in A / total outcomes = 2/4 = 1/2.

38. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Multiplying all data points by a constant scales the standard deviation by the same constant. Thus, the new standard deviation is 6 × 3 = 18.

39. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: The number of combinations is given by C(n, r) = n! / (r!(n-r)!), where n = 10 and r = 2. C(10, 2) = 10! / (2!(8!)) = 45.

40. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: The interquartile range (IQR) represents the spread of the middle 50% of the data, calculated as Q3 - Q1.

41. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Use Bayes’ Theorem: P(A | Defective) = P(A) * P(Defective | A) / P(Defective). Calculate P(Defective): (0.6 * 0.05) + (0.4 * 0.08) = 0.062. Then compute: P(A | Defective) = (0.6 * 0.05) / 0.062 = 0.4286.

42. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: First calculate the mean: Mean = (5+7+12+15+20+22)/6 = 13.5. Then calculate squared deviations, average them: Variance = [(5-13.5)^2 + (7-13.5)^2 + ... + (22-13.5)^2] / 6 = 50.67.

43. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: The reliability of the system is the product of the reliability of its components: 0.95^4 = 0.8145.

44. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: Find Q1 and Q3: Q1 = Median of {10, 15, 20} = 15; Q3 = Median of {30, 35, 40} = 35. IQR = Q3 - Q1 = 35 - 15 = 10.

45. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: Use the binomial probability formula: P(X=k) = C(n, k) * p^k * (1-p)^(n-k). n=5, k=3, p=0.5. P(X=3) = C(5,3) * (0.5)^3 * (0.5)^2 = 10 * 0.125 * 0.25 = 0.3125.

46. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: According to the empirical rule for a normal distribution, approximately 68% of the values fall within one standard deviation from the mean.

47. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: There are 13 hearts and 3 additional aces (not hearts) in a 52-card deck. Total favorable outcomes: 13+3=16; P = 16/52 = 0.325.

48. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: CV = Standard deviation / Mean. Mean = (8+12+14+16+20)/5 = 14. SD = sqrt([(8-14)^2+(12-14)^2+(14-14)^2+(16-14)^2+(20-14)^2]/5) = 4. CV = 4/14 = 0.25.

49. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Use the formula: P(A or B) = P(A) + P(B) - P(A and B). P(A or B) = 0.6 + 0.5 - 0.2 = 0.8.

50. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: The empirical rule states that 95% of values fall within two standard deviations from the mean: Mean ± 2(SD) = 25 ± 2(5) = [15, 35].

51. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: P(Green first) = 5/12; P(Green second) = 4/11. P(Both green) = (5/12) * (4/11) = 0.2273.

52. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: In a positively skewed distribution, the mean is pulled toward the tail, making it larger than the median.

53. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: Numbers divisible by both 3 and 5 are multiples of 15. Between 1 and 100: {15, 30, 45, 60, 75, 90} = 6 numbers. Probability: 6/100 = 0.08.

54. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Adding a constant to all data points does not change the standard deviation; it remains 20.

55. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: Use the binomial formula: P(X=k) = C(n, k) * p^k * (1-p)^(n-k). n=3, k=2, p=0.7. P(X=2) = C(3,2)*(0.7)^2*(0.3)^1 = 3*(0.49)*(0.3) = 0.392.

56. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: The R-squared value reflects the proportion of variance in the dependent variable explained by the independent variable(s).

57. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: This problem follows a binomial distribution with n=10 trials and p=0.03. Use the binomial probability formula P(X=k) = (nCk)(p^k)(1-p)^(n-k) to calculate the probability for k=2.

58. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: There are 13 spades in the deck. The probability of selecting the first spade is 13/52, and the probability of selecting the second spade without replacement is 12/51. Multiply these probabilities: (13/52)*(12/51)=0.0538.

59. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: To calculate the population standard deviation, first calculate the mean, then find the squared differences from the mean, and finally compute the square root of the average of these squared differences.

60. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: The probability that all components fail is (1-0.90)^3 = 0.001. Hence, the probability that at least one works is 1 - 0.001 = 0.999.

61. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: A correlation coefficient of -0.85 indicates a strong negative linear relationship between the two variables.

62. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: The probability of drawing the first blue marble is 5/14, and the probability of drawing a second blue marble without replacement is 4/13. Multiply the probabilities: (5/14)*(4/13)=0.0909.

63. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: Subtracting a constant from all data points affects the mean (mean - constant) but does not change the standard deviation.

64. Correct Answer: D
   Explanation: This follows a binomial distribution. Use the formula P(X=k) = (nCk)(p^k)(1-p)^(n-k) with n=4, k=3, and p=0.6.

65. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Standard deviation is calculated as the square root of the variance, representing the spread of data around the mean.

66. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: The probability of landing on green is the number of green pockets divided by the total number of pockets: 2/38 = 0.0526.

67. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: CV is calculated as (Standard Deviation / Mean) * 100. The mean is 6, and the standard deviation is 2. Therefore, CV = (2/6) * 100 = 40%.

68. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: The probability of rolling a single six is 1/6. The probability of rolling a non-six is 5/6. Using the binomial formula P(X=k) = nCk * (p^k) * ((1-p)^(n-k)), where n=3, k=2, and p=1/6, we calculate P(2 sixes) = 3C2 * (1/6)^2 * (5/6)^1 = 15/216.

69. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: The mean is sensitive to extreme values because it considers all data points, while the median and mode are more resistant.

70. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: Using the binomial formula P(X = k) = nCk * (p^k) * ((1-p)^(n-k)), we calculate P(X = 3) = 5C3 * (0.4^3) * (0.6^2) = 10 * 0.064 * 0.36 = 0.1568.

71. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: When data is multiplied by a constant, the standard deviation is also multiplied by the same constant. Here, 4 × 3 = 12.

72. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: The probability of all servers being functional is P(All servers working) = (0.9)^4 = 0.6561.

73. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: Sample variance is calculated as the sum of squared differences between each value and the mean, divided by n-1. Mean is 17.5, variance = [(5-17.5)^2 + (10-17.5)^2 + ... + (30-17.5)^2] / 5 = 62.5.

74. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: Using the binomial formula P(X=k) = nCk * (p^k) * ((1-p)^(n-k)), with n=5, k=3, and p=0.7, we calculate P(3 prefer A) = 5C3 * (0.7^3) * (0.3^2) = 10 * 0.343 * 0.09 = 0.3087.

75. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: The probability of both subsystems working simultaneously is P(A and B) = P(A) * P(B) = 0.8 * 0.9 = 0.72.

76. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: The dataset is symmetric, as the mean, median, and mode are equal, suggesting zero skewness.

77. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: The expected value is calculated as E(X) = n * p. Here, E(X) = 10 * 0.7 = 7.

78. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Numbers greater than 40 are {41, 42, ..., 50}, a total of 10 numbers. Probability = 10/50 = 0.2.

79. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: The probability of getting one red and one blue is P(Red, Blue) = (5/8 * 3/7) + (3/8 * 5/7) = 15/56 + 15/56 = 30/56.

80. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: CV is calculated as (Standard deviation / Mean) * 100. Mean = 110, SD = sqrt(50). CV = (sqrt(50) / 110) * 100 ≈ 5.00%.

1. Which protocol is responsible for converting IP addresses into MAC addresses in a local network?
   A) DNS
   B) ARP
   C) DHCP
   D) ICMP

2. At which OSI layer does encryption typically occur?
   A) Transport Layer
   B) Data Link Layer
   C) Presentation Layer
   D) Network Layer

   A) 255.255.255.192
   B) 255.255.255.224
   C) 255.255.255.248
   D) 255.255.255.240

4. Which of the following is a link-state routing protocol?
   A) RIP
   B) EIGRP
   C) OSPF
   D) BGP

   A) 433 Mbps
   B) 1.3 Gbps
   C) 3.5 Gbps
   D) 6.9 Gbps

   A) An attack that blocks network traffic
   B) An attack where an attacker intercepts and potentially alters communications between two parties
   C) An attack that floods the network with traffic
   D) An attack that uses brute force to guess passwords

   C) 150 meters
   D) 200 meters

   D) Data Link

45. A wireless network experiences interference from nearby devices. Which frequency band is most likely causing this issue?

   B) Store-and-forward is faster than cut-through.
   C) Cut-through requires less memory than store-and-forward.
   D) Store-and-forward switches operate at Layer 4, while cut-through switches operate at Layer 2.

   B) More efficient data encryption.
   C) A vastly larger address space.
   D) Improved network speed.

   A) DNS
   B) DHCP
   C) SNMP
   D) NAT



--- CORRECT ANSWERS AND EXPLANATIONS ---

1. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: The Address Resolution Protocol (ARP) is used to map IP network addresses to the hardware (MAC) addresses used by a data link protocol in local networks.

2. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: Encryption is commonly performed at the Presentation Layer (Layer 6) in the OSI model, which is responsible for data translation and security.

3. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: To create 8 subnets in a Class C network, 3 bits are borrowed from the host portion, leading to a subnet mask of 255.255.255.224, which provides 2^3 = 8 subnets.

4. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: Open Shortest Path First (OSPF) is a link-state routing protocol that maintains a complete map of the network topology to determine the shortest path.

5. Correct Answer: D
   Explanation: Wi-Fi 5 (802.11ac) supports a maximum theoretical data rate of up to 6.9 Gbps under optimal conditions using multiple spatial streams and wide channels.

6. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: A man-in-the-middle attack occurs when an attacker intercepts and possibly alters communication between two systems without their knowledge.

7. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: The maximum recommended length for a Cat5e Ethernet cable is 100 meters, including the patch cables.

8. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: A switch operates at Layer 2 of the OSI model and uses MAC addresses to forward frames to the appropriate port.

9. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Link-local addresses in IPv6 always start with 'fe80', and they are used for communication between nodes on the same link.

10. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: Network Address Translation (NAT) allows multiple devices on a private network to share a single public IP address, helping to conserve public IPs.

11. Correct Answer: D
   Explanation: WPA3 is the most secure wireless security protocol currently available, as it provides enhanced encryption and protection against brute-force attacks.

12. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: The 'ping' command tests connectivity between devices by sending ICMP Echo Request messages and measuring packet loss.

13. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: IPSec is widely used for secure communication in VPNs and is natively supported by most modern operating systems.

14. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: The 'AAAA' record is used in DNS to map a domain name to an IPv6 address.

15. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: A mesh topology connects every device to every other device, ensuring maximum redundancy and reliability.

16. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Differentiated Services (DiffServ) is a QoS mechanism that classifies and prioritizes traffic, allowing VoIP to receive higher priority.

17. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Platform as a Service (PaaS) provides a platform for users to deploy applications without needing to manage the underlying infrastructure.

18. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: High latency indicates a long delay in the transmission of data packets between nodes, leading to slower communication.

19. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: A proxy firewall operates at the application layer, acting as an intermediary between clients and servers to inspect and filter traffic.

20. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Serial transmission sends data bits one after the other over a single channel, making it suitable for long-distance communication.

21. Correct Answer: D
   Explanation: 192.168.1.255 is the broadcast address for the subnet 192.168.1.0/24. The router forwards the packet to all hosts in that subnet.

22. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: A firewall is a security device that monitors and controls incoming and outgoing network traffic based on predetermined security rules, preventing unauthorized access.

23. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: In a star topology, all devices are connected to a central node, typically a switch or hub. If the central node fails, the entire network could be disrupted.

24. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: OSPF (Open Shortest Path First) uses bandwidth as its primary metric to calculate the cost of a route. Higher bandwidth links are preferred.

25. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: CSMA/CD (Carrier Sense Multiple Access with Collision Detection) is used in wired Ethernet networks to detect and resolve collisions when two devices send data simultaneously.

26. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: IEEE 802.11 is the standard for wireless local area networks (WLANs) and is commonly used for Wi-Fi communication.

27. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: A subnet mask is used to distinguish the network and host portions of an IP address, enabling IP routing.

28. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Cut-through switching begins forwarding packets immediately after reading the destination MAC address, providing low latency.

29. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: TCP provides reliable data delivery by establishing connections, sequencing packets, and retransmitting lost data.

30. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: SFTP (Secure File Transfer Protocol) is used to transfer files securely over the Internet using encryption.

31. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: QoS prioritizes traffic to ensure that critical services, such as VoIP or video streaming, receive the required bandwidth and low latency.

32. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: IEEE 802.11ac offers maximum theoretical data rates of up to 1.3 Gbps in the 5 GHz band using advanced modulation techniques.

33. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: A DoS (Denial of Service) attack attempts to overwhelm a network service with excessive traffic, rendering it unusable.

34. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: The ping command tests connectivity between devices by sending ICMP Echo Request packets and waiting for a response.

35. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: RIP (Routing Information Protocol) uses distance-vector algorithms, while OSPF (Open Shortest Path First) uses link-state algorithms for routing decisions.

36. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: In a mesh topology, the number of connections is calculated as n(n-1)/2, where n is the number of devices. For 6 devices: 6(6-1)/2 = 15.

37. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: 169.254.x.x addresses are Automatic Private IP Addressing (APIPA) addresses assigned when a device cannot obtain an IP address from a DHCP server.

38. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: DNS resolves domain names into IP addresses, allowing users to access resources using human-readable names.

39. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: UDP (User Datagram Protocol) is a connectionless protocol with low latency, making it suitable for real-time applications like video streaming.

40. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: The Data Link Layer encapsulates data into frames for transmission over the physical medium.

41. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: Mesh topology offers redundancy and fault tolerance because every device is connected to multiple devices, ensuring communication continues even if one link fails.

42. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: The Dynamic Host Configuration Protocol (DHCP) dynamically assigns IP addresses to devices in a network, simplifying address management.

43. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: VLANs isolate broadcast domains, preventing unnecessary traffic and enhancing overall network security and segmentation.

44. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: The IP protocol operates at the Network layer (Layer 3) of the OSI model, where routing and addressing take place.

45. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: The 2.4 GHz band is widely used and more prone to interference from devices like microwaves and cordless phones.

46. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: BGP is a path-vector routing protocol that exchanges routing information based on paths, policies, and rules defined by autonomous systems.

47. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Carrier Sense Multiple Access with Collision Detection (CSMA/CD) is used in Ethernet networks to detect and resolve collisions when multiple devices attempt to communicate simultaneously.

48. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: CIDR allows efficient allocation of IP addresses and reduces the size of routing tables by aggregating IP prefixes.

49. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: Store-and-forward switching examines the entire packet for errors before forwarding, while cut-through switching forwards the packet immediately after reading the destination address.

50. Correct Answer: D
   Explanation: IPv6 eliminates the need for Network Address Translation (NAT) due to its vast address space, simplifying routing and addressing.

51. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Using a fiber-optic backbone reduces latency by providing faster and more reliable data transmission.

52. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: Asynchronous Transfer Mode (ATM) uses 53-byte fixed-size cells, providing high-speed and efficient data transfer in WANs.

53. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: The SNMP manager collects and analyzes data from SNMP agents installed on network devices to monitor network performance.

54. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: SSL/TLS encrypts communication between a web browser and a server, ensuring secure transmission of data.

55. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: The Ping tool sends ICMP echo requests to measure round-trip time and identify packet loss in the connection.

56. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: The Spanning Tree Protocol (STP) prevents loops in a switched network by disabling redundant paths.

57. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: Platform as a Service (PaaS) provides developers with the tools and infrastructure to build, test, and deploy applications in the cloud.

58. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: Kerberos uses tickets for secure network authentication, allowing users to prove their identity without transmitting passwords.

59. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: The hypervisor manages virtual machines and allocates resources to ensure efficient operation in a virtualized environment.

60. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: A DMZ is a network segment that isolates external-facing services from internal resources, providing an additional security layer.

61. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: Quality of Service (QoS) is specifically designed to prioritize certain types of traffic, like VoIP, to ensure minimal latency and optimal performance.

62. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: NAT allows devices with private IP addresses to access the Internet by translating their private IPs to a shared public IP address.

63. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: VLANs (Virtual Local Area Networks) allow administrators to segment network traffic based on different departments or groups, improving security and reducing broadcast domains.

64. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: TCP (Transmission Control Protocol) ensures reliable data transmission by implementing error checking, acknowledgments, and retransmission mechanisms.

65. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: The 802.11r protocol, or Fast BSS Transition, is designed for seamless handoff between access points in wireless networks, improving roaming performance.

66. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Traceroute displays the path a packet takes to reach its destination and the response times for each hop along the route.

67. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: The RSA algorithm is widely used for encryption and secure communication, particularly in public-key cryptography.

68. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: HTTPS (HyperText Transfer Protocol Secure) uses encryption protocols like SSL or TLS to securely deliver web pages to browsers.

69. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Spanning Tree Protocol (STP) is used to detect and prevent loops in switched networks by creating a loop-free topology.

70. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: A hybrid cloud model combines on-premise infrastructure with public cloud environments, offering flexibility and scalability for applications.

71. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: DHCP dynamically assigns IP addresses to devices, simplifying network configuration and reducing manual errors.

72. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: A Man-in-the-Middle (MITM) attack intercepts and alters communications between two parties without their knowledge, compromising data security.

73. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: The Internet Protocol (IP) handles packet delivery between devices across different subnetworks by using routing techniques.

74. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: A mesh topology connects devices directly to each other, providing redundancy and resilience in case of device or connection failures.

75. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: Link-local addresses in IPv6 are used for communication within a local subnet and are automatically assigned to each interface.

76. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: A MAC (Media Access Control) address uniquely identifies the physical interface of a device in a network, allowing local communication.

77. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: The ARP protocol maps IP addresses to MAC addresses, enabling communication between devices on the same network segment.

78. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: IPv6 offers a vastly larger address space compared to IPv4, supporting more devices and simplifying address allocation.

79. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Wireshark is a network protocol analyzer used for capturing and analyzing network traffic in real time to troubleshoot issues effectively.

80. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: DHCP (Dynamic Host Configuration Protocol) assigns IP addresses dynamically, preventing conflicts and errors caused by manual configurations.

   D) Logic Programming

48. In Git, what is the purpose of the 'git stash' command?
   A) To save uncommitted changes and revert to the last committed state
   B) To permanently delete uncommitted changes
   C) To merge two branches
   D) To create a new branch

49. Which of the following scheduling algorithms minimizes the average waiting time for processes in a multi-programmed environment?
   A) First-Come-First-Served (FCFS)
   B) Shortest Job Next (SJN)
   C) Round Robin (RR)
   D) Priority Scheduling

50. Which of the following is NOT a common software security vulnerability?
   A) SQL Injection
   B) Cross-Site Scripting (XSS)
   C) Buffer Overflow
   D) Normalization

   C) Adaptive Maintenance
   D) Preventive Maintenance

52. Which metric is used to measure the complexity of a program's control flow?
   A) Cyclomatic Complexity
   B) Code Coverage
   C) Function Point
   D) Technical Debt

53. In Agile, what is the primary objective of a sprint retrospective?
   A) To review and approve deliverables
   B) To plan for the next sprint
   C) To reflect on the completed sprint and identify improvements
   D) To fix bugs identified in the sprint

54. What is the primary role of a Real-Time Operating System (RTOS) in embedded systems?
   A) To increase power efficiency
   B) To manage hardware interrupts
   C) To ensure deterministic task execution
   D) To abstract hardware details from the programmer

55. Which protocol is commonly used to transmit data securely over the internet?
   A) HTTP
   B) FTP
   C) HTTPS
   D) SMTP

56. Which of the following is a disadvantage of shared memory in parallel computing?

   A) To manage memory allocation
   B) To control access to shared resources
   C) To schedule operating system processes
   D) To detect deadlock conditions

59. Which cloud service model provides a complete development and deployment environment in the cloud?
   A) Infrastructure as a Service (IaaS)

   C) Software as a Service (SaaS)
   D) Data as a Service (DaaS)

60. A software engineer discovers a critical bug in a system close to its scheduled release. What is the most ethical course of action?

   C) Fix the bug without informing the team

   C) Agile Model

68. Which of the following is the primary advantage of using a distributed version control system like Git?

--- CORRECT ANSWERS AND EXPLANATIONS ---

1. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: The Agile Model is designed for iterative development and is best suited for projects where requirements are expected to change frequently.

2. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Integration Testing focuses on verifying the interactions and data flow between integrated modules of a system.

3. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: A Stack operates on the principle of Last In, First Out (LIFO), where the last added element is the first removed.

4. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: Binary search divides the problem in half with every step, resulting in a logarithmic time complexity of O(log n).

5. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Object-Oriented Programming (OOP) focuses on creating objects that interact with one another to design software systems.

6. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: High throughput is generally associated with batch processing systems, not real-time operating systems.

7. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: The Factory Method pattern defines an interface for creating objects, but allows subclasses to alter the type of objects that will be created.

8. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Version control systems like Git are designed to track and manage changes to source code over time, enabling collaboration and rollback.

9. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: HTTPS is the secure version of HTTP, using encryption to secure communication over the internet.

10. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: A Primary Key uniquely identifies each record in a database table and ensures that no duplicate values exist.

11. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: SQL Injection is a vulnerability where an attacker inserts or manipulates SQL queries through user input, potentially compromising the database.

12. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: ROM (Read-Only Memory) is used for non-volatile storage in embedded systems, retaining data even when the system is powered off.

13. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Cyclomatic Complexity measures the number of linearly independent paths through a program's source code, helping assess its complexity.

14. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: Corrective maintenance focuses on fixing bugs and errors identified in the software after its deployment.

15. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: Continuous Integration (CI) involves frequently integrating code changes into a central repository and running automated tests to detect issues early.

16. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: The Single Responsibility Principle states that a class should only have one reason to change, ensuring a separation of concerns.

17. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: Infrastructure as a Service (IaaS) provides virtualized computing resources such as servers, storage, and networks over the internet.

18. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: Functional requirements define the specific behavior or functions of a system in response to various inputs and conditions.

19. Correct Answer: D
   Explanation: The Public Interest principle dictates that software engineers must prioritize the well-being and safety of the public in their work.

20. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: Print debugging refers to inserting print statements in the code to understand the program's execution flow and locate issues.

21. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: Data coupling occurs when modules share data through parameters. It is the weakest form of coupling and promotes modularity and flexibility.

22. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Boundary value testing focuses on the inputs and outputs of the software without knowledge of the internal code structure, which is characteristic of black-box testing.

23. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: Divide and conquer divides a problem into smaller parts, solves each recursively, and combines their results to solve the original problem.

24. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: The Open/Closed Principle states that software entities should be extendable without altering the existing code base, promoting stability and scalability.

25. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Microservices allow independent scaling of services, improving deployment scalability compared to monolithic architectures where the entire system must scale together.

26. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: ACID-compliant transactions (Atomicity, Consistency, Isolation, Durability) ensure data consistency and integrity even in the presence of errors or failures.

27. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Shortest Job Next (SJN) scheduling minimizes average waiting time as shorter processes are executed earlier, reducing the time other processes wait.

28. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: The Transport Layer is responsible for managing end-to-end communication and includes features like congestion control and reliable data transfer.

29. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: To ensure confidentiality, a message is encrypted using the recipient's public key so that only the recipient can decrypt it using their private key.

30. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: A watchdog timer resets the system if it detects a failure or unresponsiveness to ensure continued operation.

31. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Adaptive maintenance modifies software to ensure it remains compatible with a changing environment, such as new hardware or operating systems.

32. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: RESTful APIs rely on stateless communication, where each request contains all the necessary information, making the system scalable and fault-tolerant.

33. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: A private cloud is dedicated to a single organization, providing enhanced control and security over resources.

34. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: A Mutex (Mutual Exclusion) allows only one thread to execute a critical section at a time, ensuring synchronization.

35. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Linked lists can dynamically adjust their size by allocating memory as needed, unlike arrays which have a fixed size.

36. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: Functional programming emphasizes first-class functions, where functions are treated as first-class citizens and can be passed as arguments or returned.

37. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: A CPU profiler is specifically designed to analyze CPU usage and identify bottlenecks in the execution of a program.

38. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Build automation tools standardize and streamline the build process, reducing errors and ensuring consistency across builds.

39. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: Support Vector Machines (SVM) with an RBF kernel can model complex nonlinear relationships, making it suitable for classification with nonlinear boundaries.

40. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Cohesion measures how closely related the tasks performed by a module are. High cohesion indicates a module focuses on a single, well-defined responsibility.

41. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: The Requirements Analysis Phase is where the system's requirements are defined, clarified, and documented. This phase ensures all stakeholders have a clear understanding of what the software should achieve.

42. Correct Answer: D
   Explanation: Negative testing is designed to check the software's behavior when provided with invalid, unexpected, or erroneous inputs.

43. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: Redundancy ensures that the system can continue functioning even when some components fail, making it essential for fault-tolerant designs.

44. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Second Normal Form (2NF) removes partial dependencies by ensuring that every non-prime attribute is fully functionally dependent on the primary key but doesn't address transitive dependencies.

45. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Quick Sort has an average-case time complexity of O(n log n), making it highly efficient for large datasets compared to other options.

46. Correct Answer: D
   Explanation: Event-Driven Architecture is designed around the creation, detection, and response to events, making it ideal for real-time processing and asynchronous operations.

47. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Functional Programming is centered on immutability, pure functions, and the use of functions as first-class citizens.

48. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: The 'git stash' command temporarily saves uncommitted changes and allows the developer to work on a clean directory without losing progress.

49. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Shortest Job Next (SJN) minimizes the average waiting time by prioritizing tasks with the shortest execution time.

50. Correct Answer: D
   Explanation: Normalization is a database design concept, not a security vulnerability. The other options are common security vulnerabilities.

51. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: Adaptive Maintenance is performed to ensure the software continues to operate in a changing environment.

52. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: Cyclomatic Complexity quantifies the number of linearly independent paths in a program's source code, indicating its complexity.

53. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: The sprint retrospective is a meeting where the team reviews the past sprint and identifies areas for improvement.

54. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: An RTOS ensures deterministic task execution, which is critical for meeting real-time constraints in embedded systems.

55. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: HTTPS (Hypertext Transfer Protocol Secure) encrypts data using protocols such as SSL/TLS, ensuring secure data transmission.

56. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Shared memory systems require careful synchronization to avoid race conditions, making process synchronization a major challenge.

57. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: The GNU General Public License (GPL) allows users to access, modify, and distribute the source code, ensuring software freedom.

58. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Semaphores are synchronization tools used to control access to shared resources and prevent race conditions.

59. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: PaaS provides a development platform, including tools and frameworks, allowing developers to build, test, and deploy applications in the cloud.

60. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: The ethical approach is to report the bug to the project manager, ensuring transparency and accountability while addressing the issue appropriately.

61. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: The Waterfall model is best suited for projects with clear objectives, low risk, and well-defined requirements because it follows a linear and sequential approach.

62. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: In the worst-case scenario, the BST could be skewed (like a linked list), making the time complexity O(n) for searching an element.

63. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Shortest Job Next (SJN) may lead to starvation since longer processes might remain in the queue indefinitely while shorter processes are continuously prioritized.

64. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: White-box testing involves verifying the internal structure, logic, and implementation of the code, making it different from black-box testing.

65. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Second Normal Form (2NF) removes partial dependencies by ensuring that all non-prime attributes are fully functionally dependent on the primary key.

66. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: The SOLID principles aim to improve the maintainability and scalability of the software design by promoting good object-oriented design practices.

67. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: The Transmission Control Protocol (TCP) ensures reliable data transfer by establishing a connection-oriented communication and managing retransmissions if packets are lost.

68. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Distributed version control systems like Git allow developers to clone the entire repository locally, enabling them to work offline and later synchronize changes.

69. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: Functional programming is a declarative paradigm that focuses on the use of functions and avoids changing state or mutable data.

70. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: Input validation checks incoming data to ensure it is valid and safe, mitigating injection attacks like SQL injection and ensuring data integrity.

71. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Agile methodology is designed to accommodate evolving requirements and emphasizes iterative development, making it ideal for scenarios with frequent changes.

72. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Linear probing is a common technique for handling hash collisions by searching for the next available slot in the hash table.

73. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: Load testing evaluates how a system performs under high demand, ensuring it can handle extreme conditions without failure.

74. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Semaphores are used to manage access to shared resources in multi-threaded applications, preventing race conditions.

75. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: The Singleton Pattern ensures a class has only one instance and provides a global access point, commonly used in resource management.

76. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: UDP is suitable for real-time communication due to its low overhead and lack of connection establishment, making it faster for low-latency tasks.

77. Correct Answer: A
   Explanation: The JOIN operation combines rows from different tables based on a related column, enabling complex queries across relationships.

78. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: Polymorphism allows methods or functions to take multiple forms, enabling flexibility and reusability in code.

79. Correct Answer: B
   Explanation: The squash option during a Git rebase operation combines multiple commits into one, simplifying the commit history.

80. Correct Answer: C
   Explanation: Parameterized SQL queries prevent SQL injection by separating query logic from input data, making it harder for malicious input to alter queries.

PRACTICE TEST - FE ELECTRICAL & COMPUTER - ELECTROMAGNETICS

1. A point charge of 2 μC is located at the origin. What is the electric field intensity at a point located 3 meters away along the x-axis?
   A) 200 N/C
   B) 600 N/C
   C) 2000 N/C
   D) 6000 N/C

2. A plane electromagnetic wave propagates in vacuum. If the magnetic field amplitude is 5 μT, what is the corresponding electric field amplitude?
   A) 1500 V/m
   B) 150 V/m
   C) 15 V/m
   D) 1.5 V/m

3. An infinitely long straight wire carries a current of 10 A. What is the magnetic field at a point located 5 cm from the wire?
   A) 0.4 μT
   B) 4 μT
   C) 40 μT
   D) 400 μT

4. Which of Maxwell’s Equations describes the relationship between a time-varying magnetic field and induced electric field?
   A) Gauss’s Law for Electric Fields
   B) Gauss’s Law for Magnetic Fields
   C) Faraday’s Law of Induction
   D) Ampere’s Law with Maxwell’s Addition

5. In a dielectric medium with permittivity ε = 4ε₀ and permeability μ = μ₀, what is the speed of electromagnetic wave propagation?
   A) 3 × 10⁸ m/s
   B) 1.5 × 10⁸ m/s
   C) 7.5 × 10⁷ m/s
   D) 6 × 10⁸ m/s

6. A coil with 100 turns and a cross-sectional area of 0.01 m² is placed in a uniform magnetic field that changes from 0.5 T to 0 T in 2 seconds. What is the induced EMF in the coil?
   A) 0.25 V
   B) 0.5 V
   C) 2.5 V
   D) 5 V

7. At the boundary between two media, the tangential components of the electric field are related by:
   A) E₁t = E₂t
   B) E₁t/ε₁ = E₂t/ε₂
   C) (E₁t * ε₁) = (E₂t * ε₂)
   D) E₁t + E₂t = 0

8. What is the primary difference between linear and circular polarization of an electromagnetic wave?
   A) Linear polarization involves a constant amplitude, whereas circular polarization has varying amplitude.
   B) Linear polarization has a fixed direction for the electric field, whereas circular polarization rotates the electric field direction.
   C) Linear polarization occurs in dielectrics only, whereas circular polarization occurs in conductors.
   D) Linear polarization is associated with high frequencies, whereas circular polarization is associated with low frequencies.

9. Which of the following equations represents the relation between the magnetic vector potential and the magnetic flux density?
   A) B = ∇ × A
   B) B = ∇ ⋅ A
   C) B = ∇²A
   D) B = A/μ₀

10. What is the energy density of an electromagnetic field in a vacuum with an electric field magnitude of 10⁴ V/m and a magnetic field magnitude of 0.05 T?
   A) 2.5 J/m³
   B) 5 J/m³
   C) 10 J/m³
   D) 20 J/m³

11. What is the power radiated by a dipole antenna with a current of 3 A, operating at a frequency of 1 GHz, and having a dipole length of 0.5 m?
   A) 0.9 W
   B) 9 W
   C) 90 W
   D) 900 W

12. A transmission line has a characteristic impedance of 50 Ω and is terminated with a load impedance of 150 Ω. What is the reflection coefficient at the load?
   A) 0.5
   B) -0.5
   C) 0.33
   D) 0

13. A circular loop of radius 0.2 m is placed in a uniform magnetic field of 0.5 T perpendicular to its plane. If the loop is rotated 90 degrees in 0.5 seconds, what is the magnitude of the induced EMF in the loop?
   A) 0.1 V
   B) 0.2 V
   C) 0.4 V
   D) 0.5 V

14. A parallel plate capacitor is filled with a dielectric material with relative permittivity εr = 5. The plates are separated by 1 mm, and the area of each plate is 0.01 m². If a voltage of 100 V is applied, what is the capacitance of the capacitor?
   A) 0.44 μF
   B) 0.55 μF
   C) 0.45 μF
   D) 0.50 μF

15. A plane electromagnetic wave travels in a medium where the relative permittivity is 4 and the relative permeability is 2. What is the speed of the electromagnetic wave in this medium?
   A) 1.5 x 10⁸ m/s
   B) 2 x 10⁸ m/s
   C) 2.5 x 10⁸ m/s
   D) 3 x 10⁸ m/s

16. A solenoid with 500 turns per meter carries a current of 3 A. What is the magnetic field strength inside the solenoid?
   A) 1.88 T
   B) 2.26 T
   C) 3.77 T
   D) 4.71 T

17. A charged particle moves in a uniform magnetic field of 0.1 T perpendicular to its velocity. If the velocity of the particle is 2 x 10⁶ m/s and its charge is 1.6 x 10⁻¹⁹ C, what is the magnitude of the Lorentz force acting on it?
   A) 3.2 x 10⁻¹³ N
   B) 3.2 x 10⁻¹² N
   C) 1.6 x 10⁻¹² N
   D) 6.4 x 10⁻¹³ N

18. A transmission line has a length of 50 m and operates at 2 GHz. What is the wavelength of the signal in the transmission line if the velocity factor is 0.8?
   A) 6 cm
   B) 8 cm
   C) 12 cm
   D) 15 cm

19. What is the skin depth of a conductor at a frequency of 1 MHz, given that the conductivity σ is 5.8 x 10⁷ S/m and the relative permeability μr is 1?
   A) 0.065 mm
   B) 0.083 mm
   C) 0.1 mm
   D) 0.12 mm

20. Two charges, Q1 = 1 μC and Q2 = -2 μC, are separated by a distance of 0.5 m. What is the magnitude of the force between them?
   A) 0.072 N
   B) 0.144 N
   C) 0.288 N
   D) 0.36 N

21. A square loop with side length 0.1 m is placed in a magnetic field of 0.2 T. If the loop is pulled out of the field in 0.2 seconds, what is the induced EMF?
   A) 0.01 V
   B) 0.02 V
   C) 0.05 V
   D) 0.1 V

22. An electromagnetic wave propagates in a medium with ε = 2ε₀ and μ = μ₀. What is the impedance of the medium?
   A) 150 Ω
   B) 212 Ω
   C) 300 Ω
   D) 377 Ω

23. A charged particle with charge q = 2 μC and mass m = 0.01 kg is released in a uniform electric field of 100 N/C. What will be its acceleration?
   A) 200 m/s²
   B) 1000 m/s²
   C) 20,000 m/s²
   D) 50,000 m/s²

24. Which of Maxwell’s equations provides the foundation for understanding how changing electric fields produce magnetic fields?
   A) Gauss's Law
   B) Faraday’s Law
   C) Ampere-Maxwell Law
   D) Gauss’s Law for Magnetism

25. A plane electromagnetic wave propagates through a medium with ε = 3ε₀ and μ = 2μ₀. What is the wave velocity in this medium?
   A) 1.5 × 10^8 m/s
   B) 2 × 10^8 m/s
   C) 3 × 10^8 m/s
   D) 5 × 10^7 m/s

26. A rectangular loop with area 0.05 m² is placed in a magnetic field of 0.3 T. If the magnetic field increases uniformly from 0.3 T to 0.6 T in 2 seconds, what is the induced EMF in the loop?
   A) 0.0075 V
   B) 0.015 V
   C) 0.03 V
   D) 0.05 V

27. A transmission line consists of two parallel conductors spaced 10 mm apart in air. If the line operates at a frequency of 1 GHz, what is the wavelength of the signal?
   A) 0.3 m
   B) 0.15 m
   C) 0.6 m
   D) 0.75 m

28. A capacitor with capacitance C = 10 μF is charged to 100 V. What is the total energy stored in the capacitor?
   A) 0.05 J
   B) 0.1 J
   C) 0.5 J
   D) 1 J

29. A proton with charge q = 1.6 × 10^-19 C and mass m = 1.67 × 10^-27 kg enters a magnetic field of 0.2 T perpendicular to its velocity. If its speed is 5 × 10^6 m/s, what is the radius of its circular path?
   A) 0.26 m
   B) 0.52 m
   C) 1.04 m
   D) 2.08 m

30. A solenoid with 500 turns generates a magnetic flux of 0.02 Wb when a current of 4 A flows through it. What is the inductance of the solenoid?
   A) 2.5 H
   B) 5 H
   C) 10 H
   D) 20 H

31. An electromagnetic wave has an electric field amplitude of 10 V/m. What is the corresponding magnetic field amplitude in a vacuum?
   A) 3.33 μT
   B) 6.67 μT
   C) 10 μT
   D) 0.1 μT

32. A circular loop of radius 0.1 m carries a current of 5 A. What is the magnetic field at the center of the loop?
   A) 31.4 μT
   B) 62.8 μT
   C) 94.2 μT
   D) 125.6 μT

33. A dipole antenna radiates power P = 100 W at a frequency of 500 MHz. What is the wavelength of the radiated waves?
   A) 0.6 m
   B) 2 m
   C) 0.3 m
   D) 6 m

34. A conductor has a cross-sectional area of 2 mm² and carries a current of 10 A. What is the current density in the conductor?
   A) 5 × 10^6 A/m²
   B) 10 × 10^6 A/m²
   C) 1 × 10^7 A/m²
   D) 0.5 × 10^6 A/m²

35. A coil rotates in a uniform magnetic field, producing an EMF. If the rotational speed doubles, how does the peak EMF change?
   A) Halves
   B) No change
   C) Doubles
   D) Quadruples

36. A transmission line delivers power to a load impedance of 100 Ω. If the input voltage is 120 V, what is the power delivered to the load?
   A) 120 W
   B) 144 W
   C) 240 W
   D) 1440 W

37. A conductor with conductivity σ = 5 × 10^7 S/m carries an alternating current at a frequency of 50 Hz. What is the approximate skin depth?
   A) 9 mm
   B) 6 mm
   C) 4 mm
   D) 2 mm

38. A circular loop with radius 0.05 m carries a current of 2 A. What is the magnetic moment of the loop?
   A) 0.005 A·m²
   B) 0.01 A·m²
   C) 0.015 A·m²
   D) 0.02 A·m²
